# Facility 01 Update⚡ Energized, Hashing, Scaling - Cardania

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2025/03/Energized-hashing-scaling.png "Energized hashing scaling")

Facility 01 Update⚡ Energized, Hashing, Scaling
===============================================

March 15, 2025

**Attention, Citizens!**  
We have been terribly lax on out blog posting, but for those of you keeping up with us on [X](https://x.com/Cardania_HQ)
 and [Discord](http://discord.gg/cardania)
, you’ll know Facility 01 is LOOKING GOOD! **Here’s a current Facility overview:**  
  
1) **Energized and Hashing** [⚡](https://emojipedia.org/high-voltage)
  
Facility 01 was energized by the local utility co. at the end of January! That process took a while as the utility co. had to upgrade the local power lines to accommodate our power draw (~.5 Megawatts). _As a reference, our facility draws roughly the same energy load as 400-500 average American homes._ **Our locality has some of the most affordable power on the North American continent, with a base rate of $.052 kwh.** Once we achieve full scale we’ll be able to determine our actual overall mining efficiency accounting for all input costs. All-in, we estimate total facility costs ~$750K, ~80% of which is just CAPEX for mining machines, with **~$450k-$500k/yr in profit at** **sub 100K** **BTC prices.**  
_Founder’s Note:_ _To be clear, I don’t care about current prices. I built this for the next several years for the most righteous face-melting BTC gains the world will ever see._

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2025/03/Loops.mp4)  
**2) Scaling our Cooling Loops** [💧](https://emojipedia.org/droplet)

We currently have **10x/60x hydro-cooled machines fully operational on 2x cooling loops**. We had initially planned for 10x/loop but after much tinkering settled on a scalable stable design with 5x/loop. This iterative design process took ~30 days from energization. **We are now simply building out the additional loops and you can expect to see more come online in the coming weeks.** While this part is annoyingly boring, this is a critical component for scale. Hydro-cooled ASIC miners are considerably more powerful and efficient than their air-cooled counterparts, and our cooling loops ensure system efficiency and longevity.

![Hydro-Cooled ASIC cooling loop](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2025/03/PVC-loop-rotated.jpg)  
  
**3) Mining Dashboard Public Beta** [⛏️](https://emojipedia.org/pick)

The mining dashboard is **[ready for public testing and you can check it out here](https://mining-dashboard-v2.vercel.app/dashboard)
**. Note rewards are not currently calculating, but you can see how many Nexus Miners you have on both Cardano and Ordinals and you can see our live miners.

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2025/03/image-2.png)

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2025/03/image-1.png)

We expect to push this live in the next month once we get a handle on reward payouts and more machines turned on. **Note _additional bonuses_ will be available for holders of Cardania gaming NFTs in a future update once we achieve full scale.**

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2025/03/image.png)

4) **More Slots to Fill** [💰](https://emojipedia.org/money-bag)

~50% of the Facility has been filled by [**House of Titans**](https://houseoftitans.io/)
 with another ~25% filled by [**Banker Labs**](https://www.bankerlabs.co/)
. This B2B collaboration with other like-minded Cardano projects was both fortunate and necessary, as [Nexus Miner](https://nexus.cardania.com/miners)
 sales (_and more generally sales on Cardano_) have been pretty sluggish. We had originally planned to fill the whole facility with Nexus Miners ASICs but sales have not yet supported that plan – So, Nexus Miners will enjoy variable rewards **up to 10% of ALL active machines** in the facility, as well as **90% of rewards** for Cardania purchased machines. Cardania may also optionally buy out miners from our partners if/when they’d like to upgrade or relocate _(though we hope they stick around)_, giving Cardania a path to scale up as desired. Rewards will always vary based on hash difficulty, BTC price, operational and maintenance costs, etc. This is effectively a tokenized commodity derivative, so volatility is baked in.

**Nexus Miners will remain on sale until we can add no additional productive value into Facility 01!** _As of right now we estimate we can still fit more than $80K+ of mining value into Facility 01._ **Mint yours on [Cardano](https://nexus.cardania.com/miners)
 or Bitcoin Ordinals ([Ultra](https://app.inscribe.io/popup/VfhjHgmku1QH3JAR)
, [Deluxe](https://app.inscribe.io/popup/5gncEf4wNsPz9N9G)
, [Standard](https://app.inscribe.io/popup/T3fN4RyAHcfhTUDX)
) today!**

5) **Scaling & Replicating Facility 01** [⚡](https://emojipedia.org/high-voltage)

**We’d love to scale more and have been approached for a second facility site for which we have a tentative LOI in place**. However, we also understand liquidity on Cardano (and our social reach) is limited, so we will continue seeking funding where it presents itself. We have a unique opportunity to stack hashpower in the United States during the Bitcoin revolution, so we’d like to do as much of that as possible. **We’ve always said we will scale to wherever Cardano allows us, and if you guys want more mining and more facilities, we will build and deploy them.** In the meantime, we have been cooking up a new tokenized mining offering with a fresh brand for **[Solana](https://solana.com/)
** behind the scenes, which we’ll unveil in the very near future.

# Cardania Lore - Cardania

![Painted Raiders Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_back.jpg)

![Painted Raiders Foreground Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_fore.png)

Codex - Knowledge Base

Cardania Lore
=============

Hundreds of thousands of millennia ago Cardania was launched as a deep-space colonization project. An impressive Earth-like biome was constructed, supporting continuous evolution and expansion.

Numerous civilizations have risen and fallen across, around and inside Cardania. Countless calamities have befallen the structure, but she remains a habitable, albeit treacherous, place to call home.

Today, in around the year 1M CE, Cardania is a glorious, chaotic testament to the perseverance of life in the void of space.

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2022/11/Cardania1-1-1024x640-1.png)

Within the FOUNDATION sector at the very heart of the megastructure is the **[SUMMONING POOL](https://codex.cardania.com/the-summoning-pool/)
**. A mystical interdimensional portal and limitless source of energy. It also summons an endless array of creatures, magic, and trouble from the void of interdimensional space.

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2022/12/SUMN_Concept_2-1000px.png)

Ancient Cardania Lore
---------------------

In the earliest transcripts of Cardania, human colonists designed and manufactured large-scale climate control systems that would support human life in what became known as “the biome”. The primary goal was to replicate the atmospheric conditions of Earth within a self-sustainable environment. After hundreds of years of development, it finally became possible for ‘Terraforms’ to be constructed within vast terrain sectors. These Earth-like landscapes were fully supported by the advanced technology, which automatically maintained temperature, light and other conditions.

Underpinning almost everything that allows the megastructure to exist is The Quantum Dark Energy Drive is the beating heart of the Cardania megastructure. An ancient megalith that enables limited teleportation of Cardania across space, time and dimensions. The Quantum Dark Energy drive is powered primarily by the Summoning Pool. Cardania thus travels to new locations for limited excursions, though often without the control or consent of her citizens. Cardania always (eventually) returns to her anchor point in the Sol system of the material dimension.

Earth’s finest AI architects created the ‘CS1’ system to make Cardania largely self-sufficient. CS1 represents the accumulation of human-led Artificial Intelligence. The AI is extended through a network of robots to service and maintain the structure. The AI robots that provide support and aim to enhance the lives of humankind are known as ‘The Custodians’.

The Cardania biome was effectively ‘grown’ from a variety of Earth genome samples. The architectural concept for the biome was that the terraforms would provide a variety of terrains and landscapes that had existed on planet Earth. Advanced biotechnology and synthesized climates would then support as many of the species that had been recovered from Earth. The architects had celebrated their great success in achieving what was thought to be an impossible goal.

Whilst the biome is undoubtedly a marvel of science, it is also a wonder of evolution. The architects had created the perfect conditions for Earth life, yet at the same time had also paved a pathway for many new forms of life to thrive. Over many eons a wide variety of organisms emerged, evolved and prevailed. Many species that humans could never have anticipated are now competing for territory and natural resources within the vast ecosystems of Cardania. Skirmishes and battles are commonplace and periodically large-scale wars are fought. The last Great War concluded with Imperators retaking control of the Alpha sectors. Humankind now largely exists only within colonized areas of the Alpha sectors.

Humankind
---------

Through the progression of many millennia the tree of human evolution ‘forked’ a number of times. Several human subspecies emerged and prospered, whilst many withered and became extinct.  
  
Around half a millennia ago, biotechnological development made symbiosis possible between organism and machine. Initially this was limited to animals but later ‘grafters’ were performing underground human-cyborg enhancements for anyone with enough RAD to cover the ‘upgrades’. This allowed for certain individuals within society to increase their capabilities and prolong their life.

# Factions - Cardania

![Painted Raiders Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_back.jpg)

![Painted Raiders Foreground Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_fore.png)

Codex - Knowledge Base

Factions
========

Cardania is inhabited by various lifeforms. Do they always get along? Nope! But there is a balance that seems to work, most of the time… **Let’s meet the factions!**  
  
P.s. you can choose your faction in the Discord **#get-roles** channel – you get a new look and access to the faction chat channel

Custodians
----------

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2022/11/banner-custodians.png)

  

The one constant in Cardania are the Custodians, an enigmatic hive of Artificial Intelligence that tirelessly builds, repairs, and makes habitable the megastructure. The musical Custodial Intelligence A.I. consider themselves the collective caretakers of Cardania. While perhaps well meaning, the quirks of their programming and innate capacity for creation and experimentation put them at odds with many lifeforms on the station.  

Imperators
----------

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2022/11/banner-imperators4.png)

  

Imperator forces are humanity’s bulwark of civilization and prosperity in the cold and unforgiving reaches of space. While their methods may be harsh, their results speak for themselves.  
Many citizens choose to live within the relatively orderly boundaries of Imperator control. While their laws can be stringent and punishments severe, it’s a small price to pay for not being consumed by Void Worms in the wastes. Imperators are motivated by ensuring humanity survives, no matter the sacrifices that requires.  

The Fungus
----------

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2022/11/banner-the-fungus.png)

  

Cardania is home to a diverse array of sentient mycelia known collectively as “The Fungus”. A species of intelligent fungal based lifeforms that dwell primarily under the surface of Cardania.  
The Fungus is thought to be nearly as ancient as the Custodians. The Fungus enjoys a diverse evolutionary tree. Some are considered violent nuisances, while others engage with humanity as benevolent, spiritual guides. Through millennia of conflict and organic integration, the Fungus has grown mighty across the station.  

Solar Barbarians
----------------

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2022/11/banner-solar-barbarians.png)

  

In the wilds of Cardania the last remnants of an ancient galactic empire maintain a strong culture of honor and martial prowess. “The Solar” are genetically gifted, physically massive specimens of humanity. A powerful tribe of sun worshipping humans once left Earth to colonize the stars. Their civilization stretched across all of Sol, or so the stories claim – The Solar are the descendants of this once powerful empire. They now carve a tribal life in the hinterlands, enjoying the fruits of conquest and building toward the day that the Solar Empire will rise again. While considered little more than savages by the Imperators, the Solar Barbarians have a deeply rooted tribal hierarchy and honor system.  

Technomages
-----------

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2022/11/banner-technomages2.png)

  

An ancient, misbegotten race of hybrid machine organics. The Guild of Technomages have endured for nearly a millennia of Cardania’s current age. Through generations of discovery and scientific inquiry, the Technomages have unlocked many ancient mysteries of Cardania and put their discoveries to good use. They are also responsible for a number of calamities and near extinction level events. With their use of bio-enhancements, cybernetic implants, nanite injections and neural stimulants, the Technomages are arguably more machine than man. Once cursed by a machine god and now shackled to the eternal servitude of a singular directive: Assimilate all organic life.  

Void Priests
------------

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2022/11/banner-void-priests.png)

  

The enigmatic Void Priests are masters of psionic powers and manipulators of void energy. Legends hold that Cardania itself is a massive living entity of great spiritual power. For generations, the Void Priests have worshipped Cardania as nothing less than a deity. Through secretive traditions, the Priests harness raw psychic energy to create miracles and rain holy destruction upon their enemies. While reviled by their foes, they claim to serve our reality in an endless battle against unknown forces from the Void beyond…  

Spacers
-------

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2022/11/banner-spacers.png)

  

The unruly misfits and outcasts of Cardania’s human civilizations. Spacers eschew the gravity bound life and instead choose to build and run their own ships. While it is a difficult lifestyle, talented and adventurous citizens can make a good living through private trading or mining expeditions. Others earn their way through smuggling, piracy, and other such black-market work. Spacers tend to live fast and die young. Some successful spacers have managed to create their own orbital stations.  

The Darkness
------------

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2022/11/banner-the-darkness.png)

  

Paradoxically, the Summoning Pool that powers the very heart of Cardania also conjures all manner of chaotic creatures, plagues, and terrors from the Void. These creatures routinely wreak havoc across the world and have been responsible for countless calamities across time immemorial. Over time, Summoners have come to recognize a malign intelligence behind the creatures and that source is now collectively known as “The Darkness”.

# Citizens - Cardania

![Painted Raiders Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_back.jpg)

![Painted Raiders Foreground Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_fore.png)

Codex - Knowledge Base

Citizens
========

Citizens are your biosynthetic Web3 avatars designed for both 2D and 3D gamification.

There are 6,000 Citizens in the set.

**BUY HERE**  
JPG.store – [https://www.jpg.store/collection/citizens](https://www.jpg.store/collection/citizens)
  
Plutus.Art – [https://www.plutus.art/collection/citizens](https://www.plutus.art/collection/citizens)

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2023/01/Citizen-purple-1024x1024.png)

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2023/01/Citizen-green-1024x1024.png)

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2023/01/Citizen-yellow-1024x1024.png)

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2023/01/Citizen-blue-1024x1024.png)

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2023/01/Citizen-red-1024x1024.png)

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2023/01/Citizen-black-1024x1024.png)

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2023/01/Citizen-white-1024x1024.png)

Utility
-------

**Harvesting**  
Citizens increase resource token production by 25%. This would round up to the nearest whole number. So for 5 quantity it will be boosted to 7 and for 10 quantity it will be boosted to 13.  
  
**Epoch Wars**  
Citizens provide the following boosts to Terraforms stats:  
+1 defense as standard for any citizen  
+1 attack / +1 defense if the citizen’s faction affinity matches your faction  
+1 attack / +1 defense if the citizen’s faction affinity is RAD Token or RAD Pick  
+2 attack / +2 defense if the citizen’s faction affinity is The Darkness

Citizens also have utility in the [Stellar Hood](https://codex.cardania.com/stellar-hood/)
 game

Attributes & Rarity
-------------------

The first thing to mention is that 7% of Citizens have glitched metadata. The Citizens with Radio Chest instead of Communicator are super rare!

The main rarities include Gold and Chrome embellishments on the drone, helmet, belt, communicator and torches.

The Faction Affinity, Specialization, Talent and other attributes may also benefit your Citizen.

Color and gender aren’t included in the metadata. However, the serial numbers can identify color.

*   0-1800 = Yellow
*   1801-3600 = White
*   3601-5400 = Red
*   5401-7200 = Purple
*   7201-9000 = Green
*   9001-10800 = Blue
*   10801-12600 = Black

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2022/12/citizens-attributes.jpg)

Rarity tables are listed in order of ‘rarest attribute’.

# RAD Tokens - Cardania

![Painted Raiders Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_back.jpg)

![Painted Raiders Foreground Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_fore.png)

Codex - Knowledge Base

RAD Tokens
==========

**Disclaimer**  
  
_The RAD token is fundamentally an “arcade” token used for non-gambling web3 game applications. Cardania Digital Assets is a producer of web3 game experiences and digital collectibles, and RAD is intended as a token through which users may access or purchase experiences and/or collectibles, and a token through which users receive rewards._  
  
_Ownership of RAD does not grant any expressed or implied rights or privileges associated with Cardania Digital Assets, partners, or third parties. Blockchain tokens are extremely volatile, often have low liquidity, and subject to ongoing regulatory changes. We do not advise treating RAD (or any) web3 game token as an investment vehicle._  
  
_Cardania Digital Assets reserves the right to alter the utility, reward methodologies, distribution, and other parameters of the RAD token at any given time, for any reason._  
  
_Please consult with a licensed financial professional in your jurisdiction before buying or selling any cryptocurrency._

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2022/12/RADToken3-0-512px.png)

RAD token is the native currency of Cardania.

**Available supply**: 45 billion  
**Total supply**: 90 billion (45 billion burned)  
**Circulating supply:** ~9 billion

**Exchanges**: [MinSwap](https://app.minswap.org/swap?currencySymbolA=&tokenNameA=&currencySymbolB=6787a47e9f73efe4002d763337140da27afa8eb9a39413d2c39d4286&tokenNameB=524144546f6b656e73)
, [MuesliSwap](https://ada.muesliswap.com/markets/token/6787a47e9f73efe4002d763337140da27afa8eb9a39413d2c39d4286.RADTokens)
, [SundaeSwap](https://exchange.sundaeswap.finance/#/swap?swap_from=cardano.ada&swap_to=6787a47e9f73efe4002d763337140da27afa8eb9a39413d2c39d4286.524144546f6b656e73)
  
  
**Charts**: [RAD / ADA Chart (taptools.io)](https://www.taptools.io/charts?pairID=0be55d262b29f564998ff81efe21bdc0022621c12f15af08d0f2ddb1.f73964cf9bfdc80b6b1b5a313100dede92dabe681e5fa072debb8a53f798e474)

Token Utility
-------------

$RAD is a general purpose “arcade” token for the Cardania game ecosystem.

  
“**Sinks”** _Ways that RAD is taken out of circulation_  
  
**Assets** – NFTs, cards, ships, avatars, equipment, resources, etc.  
**Purchases** – Consumables, XP boosts, cosmetics, death mechanics, services, upgrades  
**Tributes** – RAD tributes for community and faction level benefits

**“Faucets”** _Ways that RAD is added into circulation. Updated 2023:_  
  
**Gameplay** – RAD will be earned through general game interactions  
**Events** – Win RAD by participating in regular community events  
**DEXs** – Secondary market purchases are available on various DEX’s

**Liquidity Pools**  
Users can currently contribute to RAD-ADA Liquidity Pools on [Minswap](https://app.minswap.org/)
. These pools are run by third party DEX’s not associated with Cardania. Defi applications have their own risks associated with them, always engage with caution.

**50% Supply Reduction:** In early 2022, 50% of total token supply (45B) was locked into a burn wallet. Future deflationary mechanisms may be developed using an organic distribution methodology which corresponds with user acquisition & retention.

# Resources - Cardania

![Painted Raiders Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_back.jpg)

![Painted Raiders Foreground Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_fore.png)

Codex - Knowledge Base

Resources
=========

We currently have 40 resource tokens that are on-chain to be used in the gaming ecosystem. There are no limits on the supply for these tokens, they will be minted as required for game balance.

NOTE: Resources will be centrally priced in RAD, and resources are of FIXED value. Its important to understand these resources are meant to be strictly functional, not speculative assets.

which defy the laws of traditional Newtonian physics.\

Toxic Waste

How do I gather resources?
--------------------------

**TERRAFORMS** – Cardania resource tokens are produced primarily by Terraforms. Resources can be harvested by wallets that are delegated to the Summoning Pool every epoch. The more Terraforms you have, the more resources you will be able to harvest. Check out which resources are produced by certain [Terraform attributes](https://codex.cardania.com/terraforms/)

**STELLAR HOOD** – [Check out our Stellar Hood partnership](https://codex.cardania.com/stellar-hood/)
 to find out about gathering Cardania resources in the Stellar Hood game.

How do I harvest resources?
---------------------------

**HARVESTING** – Once you have some resource production, you can [harvest via the Nexus](https://codex.cardania.com/harvesting/)

Want to check your wallet for missing resources? [Check out this fan tool](https://t5software.github.io/cardania-tools-prod/)
 (note this is 3rd party, not Cardania developed)

How do I use resources?
-----------------------

Resources will be used for a variety of game-based crafting and marketplace activity.  
  
Tokens can currently be traded in our Discord marketplace using the ‘Deal Seeker’ bot (Asset Exchange).  
  
Details will follow on how to use resources for in game activity – we will post links here and in the game pages themselves.

# The Summoning Pool - Cardania

![Summoning Pool Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/monster.jpg)

The Summoning  
Pool
====================

Earn Ada and $RAD with noncustodial staking.

Ticker: SUMN

Pool ID: dc508ac7975e573adf6ef17873c74d200e0cd71931c139eb76853281

Fixed Fee: 340₳ | Margin Fee: 1.99% | [\[More\]](https://cexplorer.io/pool/pool1m3gg43uhtetn4hmw79u8836dyq8qe4cex8qnn6mks5egza7n6tp)

[Stake With SUMN](https://cardania.com/the-summoning-pool/#)
 [Reward Calculator](https://cardania.com/the-summoning-pool/#)

### Live Stake

2.06M

### Delegators

1,926

### Blocks

Last Epoch

2

### Total Blocks

All Time

1,441

The Raddest Stake Pool on Cardano
---------------------------------

Delegators to SUMN are eligible to per-epoch $RAD distribution in addition to the pool’s Ada rewards. $RAD is allocated to delegators based on their active stake through the Cardania Nexus, which is also the home to [Epoch Wars](https://cardania.com/#epochWars)
, web3 RPG where you are the true owner of your rewards.

[\[Launch Nexus\]](https://nexus.cardania.com/)

![RAD Logo](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/rad.png)

$RAD, The Currency of Cardania
------------------------------

[$RAD](https://cardania.com/the-summoning-pool/#)
 is a Cardano Native Token and the principal currency of Cardania. [Terraform](https://cardania.com/#terraforms)
 owners and delegators to [SUMN](https://cardania.com/the-summoning-pool/)
 earn $RAD each Cardano Epoch and may spend it in-game on a variety of upgrades, consumables and cosmetics.

$RAD is the foundation of a dynamic in-game economy, with 7.5B $RAD in circulation and over 900M spent in-game by players.

Recent News and Updates
-----------------------

[![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2025/03/Energized-hashing-scaling.png "Energized hashing scaling")](https://cardania.com/blog/facility-01-update%e2%9a%a1-energized-hashing-scaling/)

[\[Read More\]](https://cardania.com/blog/facility-01-update%e2%9a%a1-energized-hashing-scaling/)

### [Ordinals Nexus Miners](https://cardania.com/blog/ordinals-nexus-miners/)

[\[Read More\]](https://cardania.com/blog/ordinals-nexus-miners/)

### [Nexus Miners v1](https://cardania.com/blog/nexus-miners-v1/)

[\[Read More\]](https://cardania.com/blog/nexus-miners-v1/)

Starships
---------

Starships add range, attacks/epoch and attack power when assigned to Terraforms. Starships come in 5 models with 20 variations and hundreds of possible loadouts. When you’re not attacking other Terraforms in Epoch Wars, race your starships in Nebula Run, a fun, fast-paced PvP racing game that leverages the unique attributes of each starship.

[\[MINT STARSHIPS\]](https://nexus.cardania.com/starships)

Community
---------

At its heart, Cardania is a community. Join us and see what makes Cardania the raddest destination in the Ultraverse.

# Tokens - Cardania

![Tokens Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/space_lamp.jpg)

Tokens
======

Jump to: [Currency Tokens](https://cardania.com/tokens/#currencyTokens)
 | [Game Tokens](https://cardania.com/tokens/#gameTokens)
 | [Collectibles](https://cardania.com/tokens/#collectibles)

Currency Tokens
---------------

![RAD Logo](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/rad.png)

$RAD, The Currency of Cardania
------------------------------

[$RAD](https://cardania.com/tokens/#)
 is a Cardano Native Token and the principal currency of Cardania. [Terraform](https://cardania.com/#terraforms)
 owners and delegators to [SUMN](https://cardania.com/the-summoning-pool/)
 earn $RAD each Cardano Epoch and may spend it in-game on a variety of upgrades, consumables and cosmetics.

$RAD is the foundation of a dynamic in-game economy, with 7.5B $RAD in circulation and over 900M spent in-game by players.

Resource Tokens
---------------

Cardania Terraforms produce Resource Tokens each Cardano Epoch. Resources may spend it in-game on a variety of upgrades, consumables and cosmetics. Every Cardania Resource is a Cardano Native Token that the player owns and may self-custody, trade, or sell independent of Cardania.

[\[Learn More\]](https://cardania.com/codex/resource-tokens/)

Game Tokens
-----------

Terraforms
----------

Cardania is home to 20,000 resource producing Terraform NFTs. Every Cardano Epoch, Terraforms produce $RAD and Resources based on their individual attributes. Terraforms and the $RAD and Resources they produce are player-owned Cardano native tokens.

[\[Explore Terraforms\]](https://www.jpg.store/collection/cardaniaterraforms?tab=items)

### Quest for Glory and Riches

Terraforms are the staging ground for Epoch Wars, the central conflict of Cardania. Mount attacks from your lands and enjoy the bountiful spoils of victory. Terraforms also unlock quests each epoch with rich lore and NFT loot.

### Fortify with Citadel

Invest your Terraform’s Resources into improving your battle posture with Citadel. Citadel is made up of 9 components that amplify strength, range, XP gain, and Resource acquisition.

### Extend your Reach

Amplify your range and attack power with Cardania NFTs such as [Starships](https://cardania.com/tokens/#starships)
, [Citizens](https://cardania.com/tokens/#citizens)
, [ETU Trading Cards](https://cardania.com/tokens/#etu)
, [weapons](https://cardania.com/tokens/#equipment)
, and [Ultrabots](https://cardania.com/tokens/#ultrabots)
. The assets you own and attach to your Terraforms extend their range, attack power and defensive capability.

![Fungal Terraform Spinning](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/Fungal1.gif)

Fungal Type Terraform

Mintable Loot
-------------

Each Terraform is the home base for endless adventure. Players explore nearby anomalies that reveal the lore of Cardania and contain real NFT riches. Players may mint the loot they discover for free and use it to add buffs to their in-game character, including increased attack, defense, XP gain, range and spirit. Loot items are built to spec on [Ready Player Me](https://readyplayer.me/)
 avatar sizes for potential future metaverse standards. A 3D Arena shooter is also in development.

![Fungus Armor Suit](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/F_All.png)

![Golden Gun](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/QmVqYFGiGgEYTxtZDPCq3EWnVyLAyF1WHqGLchoMoWAwsE.png)

![Solars Armor Suit](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/Solars.png)

![Diver's Helmet](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/QmZ7ZkjqjeDw83z8to487LQbZFrZM5eKgJ6js7FKhjGQWj.png)

Starships
---------

Starships add range, attacks/epoch and attack power when assigned to Terraforms. Starships come in 5 models with 20 variations and hundreds of possible loadouts. When you’re not attacking other Terraforms in Epoch Wars, race your starships in Nebula Run, a fun, fast-paced PvP racing game that leverages the unique attributes of each starship.

[\[MINT STARSHIPS\]](https://nexus.cardania.com/starships)

Citizens
--------

When assigned to Terraforms, Cardania’s Citizens add Attack and Defense and provide vital farming duties, increasing per-epoch yield.

[\[EXPLORE THE COLLECTION\]](https://www.jpg.store/collection/citizens?tab=items)

Enter the Ultraverse Trading Cards & Packs
------------------------------------------

Enter the Ultraverse is a trading card game built for the Block Chain. Payers have real ownership of their unopened packs and trading cards, granting the freedom to trade collectables freely.

### Cards

ETU cards have many uses in Epoch Wars, including [ETU Duel](https://cardania.com/games/enter-the-ultraverse/#etu-duel)
, a boss-fighting style mini-game with NFT loot. The full ETU PVP game is currently in development.

[\[View the Collection\]](https://cardania.com/codex/etu-card-library/)

![Allegan the Restorator](https://media.cardania.com/img/cards/QmaJgER42V3gwgv4tb7tqCWupekdihz9V5VpcLdPCve8j4)

### Unopened Packs

Relive the magic of youth with collectible card packs that may be opened in [Nexus](https://nexus.cardania.com/)
 to reveal 7 random cards from the collection.

[\[Learn More\]](https://cardania.com/codex/unopened-card-packs/)

Ultrabots
---------

The perfect companion to any Cardania Citizen, Ultrabots come in over 280 variations and add attack, defense, range, and XP gain when equiped from a player’s inventory. Ultrabots may also be attached to [Terraforms](https://cardania.com/tokens/#gameTokens)
 for a spirit buff that will be vital to the player in [ETU Duel](https://cardania.com/games/enter-the-ultraverse/#etu-duel)
.

[\[MINT Ultrabots\]](https://nexus.cardania.com/ultrabots)

Collectibles
------------

Founders Cards
--------------

Founders Cards were the first collectible released by Cardania. They signify a dedication to the mission of Cardania and bestow unexpected and delightful perks to holders.

[\[Learn More\]](https://cardania.com/codex/founders-cards/)

![All Founders Cards](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2023/01/Cards-Stacked.png)

![First Edition Card Art Example](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/monster.jpg)

First Edition Card Art
----------------------

An NFT Collection of art from the First Edition of Enter the Ultravers, this collection includes beautiful works from Dreamcoined, Alex F.C., Foeniculum, Paulo Gaviola, Mina, Davide Molino, John Pethick, Pvnkhzrd, RogueRaashk, Shadowpriest, Sergei Smekalov, and Nicholas Wolf.

[\[Learn More\]](https://cardania.com/codex/art/)

Attention, Citizens
-------------------

Attention Citizens is an NFT Music Album featuring incredible tracks by Frigid Beats, Jack Hammer, Quad Lazr, and TheNeverEngine. The NFT includes an on-chain media player that works within [pool.pm](https://pool.pm/asset1cdt7v388scknqwfdluxt3fk7lh4ssypnv2h79h)
.

[\[Learn More\]](https://cardania.com/codex/attention-citizens-nft-music-album/)

![Attention Citizens Album](https://media.cardania.com/img/album.gif)

![Intergalactic Postage Stamp - Gold](https://image-optimizer.jpgstoreapis.com/QmbGhuw4Rit9CPtygzgivkLP1WziLv24rCZXomML9v4BMw?width=1200)

----------------------------

An early Cardania collaboration with DBStudio featuring an artful set of stamps featuring the art of the Summoning Pool and the Ultraverse!

[\[Learn More\]](https://cardania.com/codex/intergalactic-postage-stamps/)

These Enigmatic artifacts from Cardania may be sent back into the Summoning Pool for riches beyond the redeemer's wildest imagination.

# Starships - Cardania

![Painted Raiders Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_back.jpg)

![Painted Raiders Foreground Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_fore.png)

Codex - Knowledge Base

Starships
=========

There are 20 ‘Fighter’ class Starships to collect, comprising of 5 different chassis types and 4 different models (Mark 1-4). There are 5,500 total in the collection.

MINTING NOW for 250₳ at [https://nexus.cardania.com/starships](https://nexus.cardania.com/starships)
  
  
**10% REFUND!** Use the format below and a 10% refund will be sent to the wallet in the link  
_(change **$imperator** to YOUR ADAhandle) or wallet address_  
[https://nexus.cardania.com/starships?r=$imperator](https://nexus.cardania.com/starships?r=$imperator)

  
MARKETPLACES:  
_Check policy ID 9a4579e93ba889999f91db52f8b2268541fea47b8b16d961e0f77e6d_  
[JPG.store](https://www.jpg.store/collection/9a4579e93ba889999f91db52f8b2268541fea47b8b16d961e0f77e6d)
 | [Plutus.Art](https://www.plutus.art/collection/cardaniastarships)
 | [Cardania Deal Seeker (Discord bot)](https://codex.cardania.com/asset-exchange/)

Configurations & Rarities
-------------------------

Each of the Starship models (Mark 1 to 4) has a fixed Weapon + Engine configuration.  
The rest of the attributes are variable:

*   Weapon + Engine
*   Armor
*   Shields
*   Mod Slots
*   Onboard AI
*   Sensors
*   Enhancement

Your Starship will also include a Frame which can be levelled up using $RAD for collectible rarity.  

**Model Types**

| Model | Weapon | Engine | Rarity |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Firefly MK1 | C-Beam | Quantum Groove | 10% (Common) |
| Firefly MK2 | Rocket Launcher | Quantum Groove | 7% (Rare) |
| Firefly MK3 | Rocket Launcher | Quantum Groove | 2.8% (Legendary) |
| Firefly MK4 | Obliterator | Cursed | 0.2% (Ultra) |
| Hornet MK1 | Rail Gun | Halcyon | 10% (Common) |
| Hornet MK2 | Obliterator | Cursed | 7% (Rare) |
| Hornet MK3 | Chakram | Aeonium | 0.2% (Ultra) |
| Hornet MK4 | Rail Gun | Aeonium | 2.8% (Legendary) |
| Scarab MK1 | Rail Gun | Inferis | 10% (Common) |
| Scarab MK2 | Plasma Cannon | Inferis | 7% (Rare) |
| Scarab MK3 | Twin Hydra Cannons | Quantum Groove | 2.8% (Legendary) |
| Scarab MK4 | C-Beam | Tannhauser | 0.2% (Ultra) |
| Scorpion MK1 | Twin Hydra Cannons | Graviton | 10% (Common) |
| Scorpion MK2 | Twin Hydra Cannons | Halcyon | 7% (Rare) |
| Scorpion MK3 | Plasma Cannon | Photon | 0.2% (Ultra) |

| Widow MK3 | Pulse Laser | Twin Singularity | 2.8% (Legendary) |
| Widow MK4 | Plasma Cannon | Twin Singularity | 0.2% (Ultra) |

Weapons benefits for Epoch Wars
-------------------------------

**RANGE** – Starships add a +2 range to attacks in Epoch Wars

**ATTACKS** – Weapons provide additional attacks in Epoch Wars:  
+1 attacks – Twin Hydra Cannons, Railgun  
+2 attacks – Plasma Cannon, Chakram, C-Beam, Pulse Laser, Rocket Launcher  
+3 attacks – Obliterator (Hornet MK2, Firefly MK4)

# Harvesting - Cardania

![Painted Raiders Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_back.jpg)

![Painted Raiders Foreground Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_fore.png)

Codex - Knowledge Base

Harvesting
==========

Connect your wallet to [The Nexus](https://codex.cardania.com/the-nexus/)
 and you will find the ‘Harvest Resources’ option.  
If you need help with your Web3 wallet connect – [read this guide](https://codex.cardania.com/web3-wallets/)

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2022/12/living-lands-summary-1024x784.png)

_NOTE – What you see here is a snapshot of the previous epoch. Anything you added to the wallet in the current epoch will be included in the next snapshot._

**Combined power level** – This is the accumulated power level of your Terraforms

**Founder’s Card Bonus** – you can increase the RAD yield by holding a Founder’s Card

*   10% for Red, Green, Blue
*   15% for Orange, Purple
*   20% for Black, White
*   25% for ALL colors (the Gauntlet)

**Total RAD** – this is derived from the [Living Lands](https://codex.cardania.com/living-lands/)
 formula. ‘Show me the math’ gives you the full calculation with your applied figures.

**Resources Produced This Epoch** – These are produced by your Terraforms based on the various traits (see the Terraforms page). Hover on each token to see how much of each resource has been harvested.

**Assigned Citizens** – You get 25% more tokens when a Citizen is assigned to a Terraform.

Click on the top corner of a Terraform to add or remove a Citizen

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2022/12/LL-03-Attach-citizen.png)

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2022/12/LL-04-Remove-citizen.png)

Once you have attached your Citizens you are ready to select your resources and harvest.

Each token you select will add a small amount of ADA to the harvest cost.

For all 40 tokens this will not exceed 1 ADA with current chain TX costs.

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2022/12/LL-05-select-resources.png)

To complete the harvest you will need to sign a TX to send an amount of ADA within the wallet extension.

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2022/12/LL-07-payment.png)

If you are having issues with your Web3 wallet you can opt for a manual transaction.

When your TX is complete you will see a ‘Harvest Complete’ confirmation. You’re done!

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2022/12/LL-06-harvest-complete.jpg)

# 1st Edition EtU Card Packs - Cardania

![Painted Raiders Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_back.jpg)

![Painted Raiders Foreground Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_fore.png)

Codex - Knowledge Base

1st Edition EtU Card Packs
==========================

Enter The Ultraverse First Edition Playing Cards  
  
Packs were minted in 2021 and 2022 (7,000 total)  
  
Each pack contains 3 cards from two different factions PLUS one neutral card (7 total)  

| Pack Name | Quantity | Factions Included |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Transfungalism | 1,000 | Custodians + The Fungus |
| Symbiosis | 1,000 | The Fungus + Solar Barbarians |
| Cleansing Fire | 1,000 | Solar Barbarians + Imperators |
| Technocracy | 1,000 | Imperators + Technomages |
| Dark Technologies | 1,000 | Technomages + Void Priests |
| Astral Alliance | 1,000 | Void Priests + Spacers |
| Ballad of the Cosmic Cartel | 1,000 | Spacers + Custodians |

!! If you want to buy **individual cards** you can buy them on secondary marketplaces !!  
  
JPG.store – [https://www.jpg.store/collection/cards](https://www.jpg.store/collection/cards)
  
  
Plutus.Art – [https://www.plutus.art/collection/cards](https://www.plutus.art/collection/cards)

# Terraforms - Cardania

![Painted Raiders Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_back.jpg)

![Painted Raiders Foreground Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_fore.png)

Codex - Knowledge Base

Terraforms
==========

20,000 Terraforms have been established within Cardania. 

BUY HERE: [https://www.jpg.store/collection/cardaniaterraforms](https://www.jpg.store/collection/cardaniaterraforms)

These 100m x 100m lands are imbued with a number of attributes.

There are 250 exceptionally rare terraforms in the Foundation sector. These ‘Prismatic’ lands generate Quantum Dark Energy, a resource exclusive to this land type.

All Terraforms have an embedded Power Level (1-9) which correlates to RAD production, as well as a number of resources which can be harvested by players.

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2023/01/Land-Types.png)

Land Type
---------

| Land Type | Count | Rarity | Produces |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Prismatic | 262 | 1.3% | Quantum Dark Energy (10) |
| Badlands | 926 | 4.6% | Sand (5)  <br>Stone (5) |
| Tundra | 940 | 4.7% | Ice (10) |
| Fungal | 944 | 4.7% | Fungal Spores (10) |
| Desert | 946 | 4.7% | Sand (10) |
| Artificial | 979 | 4.9% | Compacted Machinery (10) |
| Wasteland | 1,823 | 9.1% | Toxic Waste (10) |
| Volcanic | 1,912 | 9.6% | Magma (10) |
| Rocky | 3,608 | 18% | Stone (10) |
| Grass | 7,672 | 38% | Greens (10) |

Alpha Sector
------------

| Alpha Sector | Count | Rarity |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Foundation | 262 | 1.3% |
| Arshi En | 9,779 | 48.9% |
| Asama | 9,971 | 49.9% |

----------

| Atmosphere | Count | Rarity | Produces |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Cursed Nanites | 526 | 2.6% | Cursed Liquid (5) |
| Antigravity Cloud | 1113 | 5.5% | Antigravity Particles (5) |
| Custodial Nanites | 1,638 | 8.2% | Custodial Nanites (5) |
| Prismatic Motes | 2,197 | 11% | Prismatic Dust (5) |
| Fungal Spores | 3,279 | 16.4% | Fungal Spores (5) |
| None | 11,259 | 56.3% |     |

Bunker
------

A bunker provides defensive attributes for a Terraform.

| Bunker | Count | Rarity | Produces |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Cardanium Bunker | 1,217 | 6%  | N/A |
| Quantum Reinforced Bunker | 2,515 | 12.6% | N/A |
| Reinforced Bunker | 3,761 | 19% | N/A |
| None | 12,519 | 62.6% |     |

Hazardous Flora
---------------

Hazardous Flora provides defensive attributes for a Terraform.

| Hazardous Flora | Count | Rarity | Produces |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Nemesis Hydra | 349 | 1.7% | N/A |
| Melodious Mantrap | 716 | 3.6% | N/A |

# Avoiding Scams - Cardania

![Painted Raiders Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_back.jpg)

![Painted Raiders Foreground Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_fore.png)

Codex - Knowledge Base

Avoiding Scams
==============

You may be a seasoned pro, but scammers are always evolving.  
Read the below sections to better protect yourself, especially if you are new to crypto.

**TRUST NO-ONE**  
Just assume everyone is trying to scam you… Don’t trust anyone!  
Even if they seem like someone you know – scammers setup fake accounts that look similar to trusted people. If the spelling or grammar is off, this is quite often an indicator you aren’t talking to the person you think you are. Always check the age of the account and for subtle differences in the name/handle. It’s a good idea to disable DMs on your general Discord settings, only turn them on when you want to talk to someone.

**IF IT SEEMS OFF, IT’S A SCAM**  
If the price is too good to be true, it’s probably a scam. For total peace of mind use a trusted escrow like [Trading Tent](https://www.tradingtent.io/)
 – if they won’t do that then you should walk away. Never fall for the “I’m having issues with that marketplace” line. They want you to send your stuff to a wallet they control.

**PROTECT YOUR SEED PHRASE**  
The only time you ever need to add your seed phrase to a website or app is when you restore your wallet with a trusted wallet provider like Eternl/Nami. BUT please check the validity of the wallet website or browser extension you are setting up. There are ‘honeypot’ scammer websites showing up top of the list as ‘sponsored links’ on search engines or ‘promotions’ on Twitter – they look very much like the ACTUAL website you want to interact with but have a slight difference. Check out our [web3 wallet info](https://codex.cardania.com/web3-wallets/)
 if you haven’t already setup your wallet for browser connection.

**WEB3 CONNECTIONS**  
You can safely ‘connect’ your wallet to a website without entering a spending password.  
If you agree to a transaction **CHECK** it has the expected TX cost + tokens  
**NEVER** input a seed phrase to a Web3 site!

**GET HARD!**  
Get a hardware wallet. These are now Web3 compatible, nobody can access your account without confirming it with the spending passcode on the USB device. But remember – don’t keep your seed phrase stored online. Make at least 2 paper copies and keep in totally separate secret places (in case of fire you might also want to use a fireproof box).

* * *

**Example Scams**
-----------------

**MOD IMPERSONATION**  
A scammer will try to DM you posing as a mod or project owner. They will converse with you 1:1 as if they are saying hello, asking for a trade or providing help.

**TRADE ESCROW**  
You are trading a token and they have a problem with using the marketplace, they will ask you to use their ‘preferred website’ for escrow. It is a scam, stick to marketplaces or well-known escrow providers if you aren’t 100% sure – it’s worth paying the fees.

**FAKE WEBSITE**  
More advanced scammers will setup fake websites that appear identical to real ones, with a slightly different web address. Before you ever mint or sign a TX – you should check the URL with a trusted Twitter account or Discord server. Never enter your seed phrase to a website you aren’t 100% sure is trusted.

# Epoch Wars Beginners Guide - Cardania

![Painted Raiders Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_back.jpg)

![Painted Raiders Foreground Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_fore.png)

Codex - Knowledge Base

Epoch Wars Beginners Guide
==========================

When you first join Cardania and begin to play Epoch Wars, your terraform will be without attack capability. So you will need to add one or more ‘attack tokens’ to wage war on other terraforms.

If your range and attack strength is poor you will need to find targets with a POORLY GUARDED defense. Terraforms without Hazardous Flora or Bunker are what you should look for. These attributes are shown within the green box on the image. You will see this view when you hover over the terraform square on the map.

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/02/image-5.png)

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/02/choose-a-target.png)

If you think you can defeat the defenses, then take a look at the resources available. The ‘underground’ blue area shows primary and secondary minerals, whilst the ‘overground’ area shows all other attributes. In this example there is a **Timelost Lithoglyph**, which yields the very rare “Timelost Runes” as a reward. Plus several others as well…. Go for it!

Take a look at the [Terraforms](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/codex/terraforms/)
 page for the various attributes and the resources they produce.

Need to Level Up Your Terraform?

Also check out this example attack video (Nexus v1.5 Mar 2023)

# Living Lands - Cardania

![Painted Raiders Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_back.jpg)

![Painted Raiders Foreground Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_fore.png)

Codex - Knowledge Base

Living Lands
============

The ‘Living Lands’ formula was launched in Epoch 324 (March 2022). At the time is was a **revolution** for NFT gaming. It has evolved to be one of the most advanced smart contract based hold-to-earn and play-to-earn solutions available in Web3.  
  
Cardano’s unique EUTxO model and stakepool technology makes it possible to regularly ‘harvest’ tokens produced by Terraform NFTs. These frequent, token heavy transactions are **prohibitively costly on other blockchains** but on Cardano the experience is seamless and **costs just fractions of a dollar.**   
  
[Harvesting](https://codex.cardania.com/harvesting/)
 of tokens can be done every epoch via the Nexus. You can gather up to 40 different Cardania resources based on your terraform attributes – [Terraform info (attributes/resources)](https://codex.cardania.com/terraforms/)
.  
  
For a small amount of ADA, you will receive the following tokens in return:

| Token | Unlocked by |
| --- | --- |
| RAD | Terraforms (Power Level) + ADA |
| Energy | Terraforms (Quantum Flux) |
| Resources | Terraforms (other attributes) |
| Partner tokens | ADA |

* * *

Boost your Returns!
-------------------

  
**$RAD Boost** – Add Founder’s Card  
  
Adding a Founder’s Card to your wallet to boost your POWER LEVEL  
  
10% – Red, Blue or Green  
15% – Orange or Purple  
20% – Black or White  
25% – All colors (‘The Gauntlet’)  

**$RAD Boost** – Attack another terraform  
  
You can boost your $RAD income when you successfully attack your neighbors. This usually gives an additional 5-10%, depending on how successful you are at attacking! Check out [Epoch Wars](https://codex.cardania.com/epochwars/)
 to see how to do this…

  
**Harvest Boost** – Add citizens  
  
Assign a Citizen NFT to your Terraform to boost RESOURCE production by 25%  
_Only one Citizen per Terraform. Excludes RAD and energy_  
  
Attributes producing qty 5 resources will be boosted to 7.  
Attributes producing qty 10 resources will be boosted to 13.

* * *

Maximise your $RAD Pickup – by Bagboy
-------------------------------------

  
The variables within your control are:  
– How much power level do you have?  
– How much ADA are you staking?  
– Are you playing EpochWars?  
  
The variables out of your control are:  
– The SUMN average delegation  
– The number of blocks SUMN got for the epoch

Check out the Whale Scale table below to see how much $RAD you can expect from your holdings.  
Examples will be based on a SUMN delegation of 5 million ADA / 2000 delegators

| Whale Scale | ADA | Power Level | Blocks | $RAD |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Broke AF | 10  | 10  | 1   | 338 |
| Broke AF | 10  | 10  | 8   | 996 |
| Terraform hodler | 10  | 100 | 1   | 3,342 |
| Terraform hodler | 10  | 100 | 8   | 9,670 |
| Stake & bake | 20,000 | 0   | 1   | 8,000 |
| Stake & bake | 20,000 | 0   | 8   | 64,000 |
| Whale hello there! | 10,000 | 500 | 1   | 20,688 |
| Whale hello there! | 10,000 | 500 | 8   | 80,188 |
| ADA poor, Terra rich! | 10  | 750 | 1   | 25,035 |
| ADA poor, Terra rich! | 10  | 750 | 8   | 72,313 |

  
Note! There are ‘modifier’ variables within the formula that are used for balancing… But I won’t complicate things by trying to explain with those. Just be aware the weighting can change from time to time between Terraform power level, ADA staking and the amount of blocks the Summoning Pool conjures.  
  
GAMING was introduced some time after the initial harvesting function. So by playing the EpochWars game you can now pickup a lot of additional $RAD every epoch from gameplay. This is achieved by using your terraforms with other tokens to attack neighbors and benefit from their terraform’s power level, quantum flux and resources.

  
**In summary!  
**– You get the most benefit from Terraforms  
– Terraforms can also be used to earn $RAD in EpochWars  
– Returns improve if SUMN produces more blocks  
– Returns adjust slightly with the average delegation  

* * *

Full ‘Living Lands’ formula:
----------------------------

Previous Epoch: 420
Delegation Score \[D\] = Total Delegation / Total Delegators
Delegation Score Modifier \[Dm\] = 0.065
Delegation Score Total \[Dt\] = \[D\] x \[Dm\]
Block Score \[B\] = Total blocks produced in prior epoch
Block Score Modifier \[Bm\] = 60
Block Score Total \[Bt\] = \[B\] x \[Bm\]
Total Score \[T\] = \[Dt\] + \[Bt\]
Land Constant \[LC\] = 0.15
Founder's Bonus \[FB\] = A bonus for Founder's card holding (25%)
Land Modifier \[L\] = individualized NFT encoded modifier score between 1-9 + FB
Efficiency \[E\] = RAD produced vs. potential due to lack of harvesting in previous epochs (100% for this epoch)
-----------
Delegator's Score \[DS\] = Delegator's Active Stake Last Epoch / SUMN Total Active Stake Last Epoch
Delegator's RAD \[DR\] = ( \[B\] \* 2000000 ) \* \[DS\]
-----------
RAD Distribution \[R\] = ( ( \[T\] x ( \[LC\] x \[L\] ) ) + \[DR\] ) \* \[E\]

RAD from spoils (successful attacks): $$$

# Epoch Wars FAQs - Cardania

![Painted Raiders Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_back.jpg)

![Painted Raiders Foreground Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_fore.png)

Codex - Knowledge Base

Epoch Wars FAQs
===============

*   **Q: I delegated my wallet, why doesn’t it show up?** A: When you delegate to a new stake pool, the delegation takes 2 full epochs to become active. So it will take 5-10 days.

*   **Q: I moved a terraform into my wallet, why doesn’t it show up?** A: An Epoch Wars snapshot is taken at the start of each epoch. Terraforms that move wallets cannot be used until the following epoch, to prevent them being used more than once. This includes Terraforms bought from a marketplace.

*   **Q: I have a terraform but I can’t attack with it, why not?** A: Each terraform requires a token to activate it’s attack capability. If the attack button is greyed out, you may be trying to attack a Terraform from the same faction. This is not allowed!

*   **Q: I added a support token to my wallet, but I can’t see it, why not?** If you add tokens to the wallet, you can ‘Rescan Wallet’ from the Harvest page. They will then show up in your inventory.

*   **Q: I bought an Enter the Ultraverse card but can’t attack with it, why not?** A: The attack function is provided by Creature and Weapon Cards only. You may have bought a Spell Card? You can check the [Public ETU Card Library](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1iDTrVb58BtKcBByKTrAs6Aa5VlmRtDhWIr3oVE2vDwI/edit?usp=sharing)
     sheet and filter for creature + weapon card types

# Epoch Wars - Cardania

![Painted Raiders Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_back.jpg)

![Painted Raiders Foreground Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_fore.png)

Codex - Knowledge Base

Epoch Wars
==========

**Epoch Wars** has the accolade of being one of the very first multiplayer games on the Cardano blockchain. Debuting in March 2023 to around 500 active players it became an instant hit.

The premise of the game is that [SUMN](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/the-summoning-pool/)
 delegators with [Terraform](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/codex/terraforms/)
 tokens can participate in battles once every epoch (5 days). Successful battles return [$RAD](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/codex/rad-tokens/)
 and [resource](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/codex/resource-tokens/)
 tokens. Plus, if you are lucky, you may find an [Anomaly](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/codex/anomalies/)
 and win a mintable NFT.

There is zero-skill required to play Epoch Wars, but a strategic mind will be of great benefit.

> **What are the returns for playing?**
> 
> Players earn variable rewards based on their activity, strategy, skill, and luck in game. We’ve engineered a system that generously rewards players for their gameplay, and also integrates passive rewards which are often quite robust.

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/02/image-1.png)

**Levelling Up Terraforms**
---------------------------

In order to achieve greatness, you will need to increase the range, attack and defense capabilities of your Terraform. Range and attack enhancements improve your ability to defeat your foes. Whilst defense helps resist their advancement.

Building a [Citadel](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/codex/citadels/)
 on your terraform will increase range, attack and defense. You can also unlock advanced features such as Research, Crafting and Spells.

_Note that Citadels can be built with the $RAD and resources earned through harvesting!_

You can also add various Cardania tokens (and tokens from other select Cardano projects) as ‘buffs’ to your personal profile, which improve your Epoch Wars capabilities.

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/02/L3-Citadel.png)

Start Playing
-------------

This is what you need to start playing EpochWars:

1.  A web3 wallet actively **delegated to SUMN** pool
2.  A **terraform** within the wallet, plus **an attack token**:
    *   Starship
    *   Citizen
    *   Enter the Ultraverse ‘creature’ card

You can use your terraform to attack once every epoch (5 days). At the turnover of each epoch terraforms will be randomly shuffled on the map, and attacks will be reset.  

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2023/03/image-3.png)

Attacking & Defending
---------------------

Carry out an attack via the **Terraform Map** page:

*   Scroll into the map using Shift + Mouse wheel up
*   Select your terraform and then ‘Mount Attack‘
*   Select a neighboring terraform to attack (note their defense rating)
*   Select Attack to initiate the battle (this will result in Victory or Defeat)
*   You cannot attack a terraform from your own faction
*   After attacking your terraform will change to a ‘Resting’ state

When attacking, you will be given an estimate chance of success. You get more Victory Points for attacks with lower chance of success:

*   1 point – Certain, High, Fair
*   3 points – Moderate, Low
*   10 points – Very low, Impossible

Terraforms will defend themselves automatically. Your terraforms will gain defense points from Hazardous Flora and Bunker attributes, but it will not lose any $RAD or resources if they are defeated.  

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/02/image.png)

The Leaderboard
---------------

The leaderboard shows the seven ‘factions’, each with a total member count and the percentage that is attributed to ‘balancing’ which can increase or decrease your experience points (XP). If you choose a less popular faction, you will increase your XP return.

The leaderboard also shows the current Epoch, with a progress bar and the current leaders for highest overall attack and defense scores. Also the ‘heroic’ members who’s terraforms have produced the most unlikely attack or defense successes. These leaders are automatically rewarded with NFT prizes at the end of the Epoch.

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/02/EpochWars-leaderboard.png)

**Faction Boosts**
------------------

You can give your faction a lift by paying 300k $RAD and 1 QDE for one of the following boosts  
– Blessing +5% XP boost  
– Bloodlust +1 Attack boost  
– Reinforcements for +1 Defense boost

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2023/06/image-1024x276.png)

# Epoch Wars Token Utility - Cardania

![Painted Raiders Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_back.jpg)

![Painted Raiders Foreground Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_fore.png)

Codex - Knowledge Base

Epoch Wars Token Utility
========================

Various Cardania tokens can be used within the Epoch Wars game – see the table below for details.

Note also, that building a [Citadel](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/codex/citadels/)
 adds various buffs to the Terraform that improve it’s capability.

| Token | Application & Unlocks | Utility |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [Starship](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/codex/starships/) | Per Terraform (1 slot) | +2 Range  <br>+1-3 Battles  <br>+3 Attack  <br>+3 Defense |
| [Citizen](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/codex/citizens/) | Per Terraform (1 slot) | +1-2 Attack  <br>+3 Defense  <br>+25% resource harvest |
| [Trading Cards](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/codex/etu-card-library/)<br>\* | Per Terraform (5 slots) | +0-10 Attack  <br>+0-10 Defense |
| [Equipment](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/codex/equipment/)<br>\*\* | All Terraforms (9 slots)  <br>Unlock Armor & Weapon at XP level 5  <br>Unlock Amulet at XP level 10  <br>Unlock Ring at XP level 15 | +0-3 Range  <br>+0-9 Attack  <br>+0-9 Defense  <br>+0-10% XP Gain |
| Trinkets\*\* | All Terraforms (5 slots)  <br>Unlock slot 1 at XP level 10  <br>Unlock slot 2 at XP level 20  <br>Unlock slot 3 at XP level 30  <br>Unlock slot 4 at XP level 40  <br>Unlock slot 5 at XP level 50 | +0-2 Range  <br>+0-2 Attack  <br>+0-2 Defense  <br>+0-10% XP Gain |
| Companion\*\* | All Terraforms (1 slot)  <br>Unlock at XP level 10 | +0-2 Range  <br>+0-3 Attack  <br>+0-5 Defense  <br>+0-10% XP Gain |
| Vehicle\*\* | All Terraforms (1 slot)  <br>Unlock at XP level 20 | +0-2 Range  <br>+0-2 Attack  <br>+0-2 Defense  <br>+0-2% XP Gain |

  
\* [Enter the Ultraverse](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/codex/enter-the-ultraverse/)
 creature/weapon cards (+attack +defense per the card). Use the [Card Library](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/codex/etu-card-library/)
 or the [ETU Cards](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1iDTrVb58BtKcBByKTrAs6Aa5VlmRtDhWIr3oVE2vDwI/edit#gid=0)
 public sheet to check for stats

\*\* All Equipment, Trinkets, Companion and Vehicle tokens can be unlocked and enabled in your player profile. These items apply to ALL your Terraforms! (not just one).

# Cardania Quick Start - Cardania

![Painted Raiders Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_back.jpg)

![Painted Raiders Foreground Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_fore.png)

Codex - Knowledge Base

Cardania Quick Start
====================

Cardania is a Web3 NFT gaming ecosystem, building began on the Cardano blockchain in 2021 with a simple ethos;

“_Long-term focus, deployment of Cardano’s best tools and features, plus a fun and real community._“

The Cardania project is totally independent. Having no third-party investment means we can develop freely and without burden. We are also not overcommitted with burdensome operating costs, this has been key to survival through an 18-month bear market. We are now nicely positioned to continue building a gaming ecosystem for Cardano web3 gaming enthusiasts.

Cardania is currently centred around two games:

*   **[Epoch Wars](https://codex.cardania.com/epochwars/)
    ** – A tile-based land strategy & battle game
*   **[Enter the Ultraverse](https://codex.cardania.com/enter-the-ultraverse/)
    ** – a PvP Trading Card Game (similar to Hearthstone and Magic The Gathering)

Epoch Wars is live today and being played by hundreds of players every epoch.

Whilst the full ‘Enter The Ultraverse’ game is being developed, we have deployed a ‘boss battle’ within Epoch Wars that uses the First Edition trading cards.

How do I join?
--------------

Here are the basic steps to being able to harvest and play Epoch Wars every epoch:

1.  Change your wallet stake to [SUMN ‘The Summoning Pool’](https://codex.cardania.com/the-summoning-pool/)
     (wait 5-10 days)
2.  Acquire a [Terraform](https://codex.cardania.com/terraforms/)
     then check out [Harvesting](https://codex.cardania.com/harvesting/)
     and [Epoch Wars](https://codex.cardania.com/epochwars/)
    
3.  Earn [$RAD](https://codex.cardania.com/rad-tokens/)
     tokens and [resource tokens](https://codex.cardania.com/resource-tokens/)
     every epoch (these are all on-chain)

**Harvesting** – If you want to bolster your harvest, you can add these buff tokens:

1.  [Founder’s Card](https://codex.cardania.com/founders-cards/)
     – Boost your [$RAD](https://codex.cardania.com/rad-tokens/)
     token harvest by 10%-25% (per wallet)
2.  [Citizen](https://codex.cardania.com/citizens/)
     – Boost your [resource](https://codex.cardania.com/resource-tokens/)
     token harvest by 25% (per terraform)

**Epoch Wars** – If you want to earn more RAD and resources in [Epoch Wars](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/codex/epochwars/)
, you can attack other terraforms. To be successful you will need attack capability. Check out the [Epoch Wars Token Utility](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/codex/epoch-wars-token-utility/)
 page.

**What is the community like?** – Cardania has the following numbers:

*   13k+ Twitter followers
*   5k+ Discord members
*   3k Terraform token holders
*   2k delegators to SUMN stake pool
*   500 regular Web3 game participants

This is a great foundation for a Web3 independent gaming platform!  

**A final word about our team**

Chris (aka “Cap”) founded the Cardania project in 2021. The eUTXO model was the catalyst for his vision to create a Web3 gaming platform with interchangeable tokens.

_Fun fact… Chris was a Captain in the US Army – hence the name ‘Cap’_

Eustacia is our Lead Developer and joined the project very early on. Without doubt Eus is one of the finest devs on the blockchain. Quietly delivering web3 minting, staking, gaming applications to a very high standard.

Behind the scenes there are several designers, artists, writers and mods all dutifully looking after Cardania. Just like the Custodian AI on the space station!

# UTxO Management - Cardania

![Painted Raiders Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_back.jpg)

![Painted Raiders Foreground Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_fore.png)

Codex - Knowledge Base

UTxO Management
===============

If you harvest regularly you will end up with a bunch of tokens in your wallet spread across multiple UTxOs (RAD, resources, etc). This is UTxO fragmentation…. Like having a lot of loose change in various pockets.

When it comes to spending $RAD on an inventory item, your wallet may need to pull tokens from various UTxOs. The problem this might cause is overloading the 16kb max TX size limit for the wallet TX. You will see the error below in this situation.

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2023/09/image-4.png)

Eternl shows your UTxOs and you can go an have a look at them all individually…

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2023/09/image-1.png)

So how do we fix it?
--------------------

  
You can combine the $RAD + ADA into a single UTxO by sending it to your own wallet address. When you do this it is a good idea to send more than minimum ADA with the transaction. E.g. send 10ADA along with the $RAD so that there will also be ample ADA on the resulting UTxO.

If you are unable to consolidate all of your RAD in a single transaction (for the same reason it’s hitting the max size limit in Nexus), you can send smaller amounts of $RAD multiple times, the end result will be a single UTxO with all your $RAD in the wallet.

If you now try again to mint with $RAD, it should work smoothly.

**Eternl ‘UTxO Collection**‘

A simple way to fix this issue with Eternl wallet is to use the ‘UTxO Collection’ option to automatically consolidate the same tokens onto a single UTxO. **(Send > Options > UTxO Collection**) – easy peasy.

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2023/09/image-5.png)

After the UTxO collection completes, you can see the difference in **Account > UTxO List**

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2023/09/image-3.png)

# Web3 Wallets - Cardania

![Painted Raiders Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_back.jpg)

![Painted Raiders Foreground Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_fore.png)

Codex - Knowledge Base

Web3 Wallets
============

The concept for Web3 wallets is that certain sites will be ‘blockchain enabled’. Look out for this being labelled as ‘Dapp’ (decentralized app). So if the site is Dapp enabled, you can connect your Web3 wallet.

Connecting your Web3 wallet to a Dapp website is similar to logging into a website using your Google or Apple account. But rather than sharing your name and profile pic, you are sharing your wallet contents.

If you have setup a Cardano native wallet like Eternl or Nami you already have a Web3 wallet.

The Nexus currently supports Eternl, Nami, Flint and Typhon. These Web3 wallets require Chrome-based browser extensions (Chrome, Edge, Brave and Opera). Mobile browsers don’t currently support Web3 wallet extensions, so there are no mobile Dapps yet.

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2022/12/Web3-Connect.png)

Safety Tips!
------------

1.  Never enter your seed phrase to a Web3 site – scammers will setup honeypot sites making it look like you are linking your wallet to their app, but they will use it to drain your wallet…
2.  NEVER ENTER YOUR SEED PHRASE TO A WEB3 SITE!!!
3.  NEVER ENTER YOUR SEED PHRASE TO A WEB3 SITE!!!
4.  Check the browser extension you are installing is legitimate
5.  You will be asked to enter your SPENDING PASSWORD, but check that fees are zero

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2022/12/eternl-extension.jpg)

Some tips on your Cardano wallet, plus hardware and web3 wallets:

*   Your ADA and tokens live on the blockchain, not in a specific wallet app. Think of a wallet app as a front end for your account on the blockchain.
*   You can ‘restore’ your account to multiple different wallets. You may want different wallet apps in case of a bug issue, or for use on a mobile app.
*   You should use a hardware wallet (cold wallet) which works for web3 in conjunction with certain web3 wallet apps that support your hardware wallet

# Equipment - Cardania

![Painted Raiders Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_back.jpg)

![Painted Raiders Foreground Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_fore.png)

Codex - Knowledge Base

Equipment
=========

With **Cardania Equipment** you will be able to navigate the metaverse with style! … And firepower!

All Cardania Equipment is housed under the “Cardania Equipment” policy ID in JPGStore! [https://www.jpg.store/collection/cardaniaequipment](https://www.jpg.store/collection/cardaniaequipment)

Policy ID: 23d9e14f176a6bf98ac5a7b5a3f00d35feeb779e3089f8cfdde70c6e

What does equipment do?
-----------------------

Equipment is usable as ‘buffs’ within Cardania games:

*   Attack / defense – usable in Epoch Wars battles
*   Spirit – usable in Epoch Wars creature card battles
*   XP gain – improve your XP rewards

\* See the list of equipment below for item buffs and collection sizes

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2023/12/image-5.png)

  
You will also be able to use equipment within [Ready Player Me](https://readyplayer.me/)
 compatible metaverses.

How do I get them?
------------------

Buy within your Nexus profile

*   Win from a [Anomalies](https://codex.cardania.com/anomalies/)
     within Epoch Wars battles
*   Buy via NFT marketplaces like [JPG Store](https://www.jpg.store/collection/cardaniaequipment)

# Stellar Hood - Cardania

![Painted Raiders Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_back.jpg)

![Painted Raiders Foreground Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_fore.png)

Codex - Knowledge Base

Stellar Hood
============

Cardania partnered with Stellar Hood in 2022, with agreements to integrate resources and also the use of Citizens within the Stellar Hood game.

Stellar Hood includes around 2,800 stars and 3,700 planets within the ‘Sol system’ (our galaxy). Each star and planet is an NFT which has been allocated Cardania resources that are available for harvesting.

Harvesting can be achieved by purchasing Stellar Hood Starbase NFT items. Once you have a Starbase you can login to the game (via Discord) and register your wallet.

Citizens and Starships can be added to a Starbase and provide certain benefits.

A word of warning, this game does require some brainpower!  
  
Website here – [https://stellarhood.com/](https://stellarhood.com/)

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2023/01/image-1-1024x632.png)

# Founder's Cards - Cardania

![Painted Raiders Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_back.jpg)

![Painted Raiders Foreground Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_fore.png)

Codex - Knowledge Base

Founder’s Cards
===============

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2023/01/Cards-Stacked.png)

Collection Info
---------------

There are 10,000 Founder’s Cards in 7 colors with 3 rarity levels:

| Card Color  <br>(JPG.store link) | Quantity | Rarity | Utility Bonus\* |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [White](https://www.jpg.store/asset/ccb3577601d6cf0e021288871112926338bee685c6c37eeadf6dddd943617264616e6961466f756e6465725768697465) | 250 | 2.5% | 20% |
| [Black](https://www.jpg.store/asset/ccb3577601d6cf0e021288871112926338bee685c6c37eeadf6dddd943617264616e6961466f756e646572426c61636b) | 250 | 2.5% | 20% |
| [Purple](https://www.jpg.store/asset/ccb3577601d6cf0e021288871112926338bee685c6c37eeadf6dddd943617264616e6961466f756e646572507572706c65) | 1,000 | 10% | 15% |
| [Orange](https://www.jpg.store/asset/ccb3577601d6cf0e021288871112926338bee685c6c37eeadf6dddd943617264616e6961466f756e6465724f72616e6765) | 1,000 | 10% | 15% |
| [Green](https://www.jpg.store/asset/ccb3577601d6cf0e021288871112926338bee685c6c37eeadf6dddd943617264616e6961466f756e646572477265656e) | 2,500 | 25% | 10% |
| [Blue](https://www.jpg.store/asset/ccb3577601d6cf0e021288871112926338bee685c6c37eeadf6dddd943617264616e6961466f756e646572426c7565) | 2,500 | 25% | 10% |
| [Red](https://www.jpg.store/asset/ccb3577601d6cf0e021288871112926338bee685c6c37eeadf6dddd943617264616e6961466f756e646572526564) | 2,500 | 25% | 10% |
| **ALL COLOURS a.k.a. “The Gauntlet”** | **250 (max)** | **Super Rare** | **25%** |

Utility Bonus
-------------

The Founder’s Cards are the first Cardania collection, released in mid 2021. So they will always have OG value and holder benefits.

Within the Nexus, the Founder’s Cards offer harvesting uplift from 10-25% and also discounts on card levelling with the same effect.

Past Airdrops
-------------

In December 2021 every Founder’s Card received a Terraform (10,000 airdropped). Then in March 2022, wallets with 7 founder’s card colors received a Prismatic Terraform (~250 airdropped).

# The Summoning Pool - Cardania

![Painted Raiders Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_back.jpg)

![Painted Raiders Foreground Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_fore.png)

Codex - Knowledge Base

The Summoning Pool
==================

The Summoning Pool is at the very heart of Cardania. It paradoxically powers the enormous space station, whilst occasionally summoning an array of creatures, magic, and trouble from the void of interdimensional space.

The **SUMMONING POOL \[SUMN\]** stakepool on the Cardano network. [Click here to see current on-chain activity from SUMN!](https://cexplorer.io/pool/pool1m3gg43uhtetn4hmw79u8836dyq8qe4cex8qnn6mks5egza7n6tp)

Citizens should stake their wallet to the SUMN to begin playing games and earning [$RAD](https://codex.cardania.com/rad-tokens/)
. This initial delegation takes a full 2 epochs (10 days or less) to complete. Then by participating in games, citizens can unlock and enjoy further benefits. Once a citizen acquires terraform lands they can earn $RAD and resource tokens every epoch.

![](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2022/12/SUMN_Concept_2-1000px.png)

# What is The Nexus? - Cardania

![Painted Raiders Background Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_back.jpg)

![Painted Raiders Foreground Image](https://media.cardania.com/assets/2024/01/codex_fore.png)

Codex - Knowledge Base

What is The Nexus?
==================

The [Nexus](https://nexus.cardania.com/)
 is a Web3 hub for Citizens to connect and engage with the Cardania ecosystem.

It works by checking all SUMN staked wallets for ADA and Cardania assets at the start of the epoch. Players who connect these wallets can then use their assets to play Cardania games.

The system is non-custodial, meaning you keep all the assets and we just take a ‘snapshot’. The inventory will be locked for the epoch, so any tokens that move wallets mid-epoch will not affect the snapshot. However, you can opt to ‘re-scan’ your wallet at any time to pick up certain game tokens like Starships and Citizens.

Staking Returns
---------------

If you are staked to [SUMN](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/codex/the-summoning-pool/)
 you can harvest every epoch. You need a [Web3 wallet browser extension](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/codex/web3-wallets/)
 to ‘connect’ your blockchain wallet.

You will get an amount of [$RAD](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/codex/rad-tokens/)
 simply for staking to SUMN (in addition to the normal ADA rewards). You can check your expected returns using our [calculator](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/the-summoning-pool/)
.

[Founder’s Cards](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/codex/founders-cards/)
 provide a 10-25% yield return boost for $RAD depending on the rarity.

Your harvest will also include bonus loot tokens (see our [partner projects](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/codex/partner-projects/)
 page for details).

Gaming Returns
--------------

The largest $RAD yield increases will be achieved through playing our games. After all, we are a gaming ecosystem that thrives on player engagement!

You can enable the [Epoch Wars](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/games/epoch-wars/)
 game by acquiring one or more [Terraforms](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/codex/terraforms/)
 and attaching other tokens:

*   [Citizens](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/codex/citizens/)
     – boost resource production by 25% + enable attack/defense
*   [Starships](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/codex/starships/)
     – enable attack/defense + increase range by 2
*   [EtU Creature Cards](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/codex/etu-card-library/)
     – enable attack/defense

The returns from attacking other terraforms are detailed in the [Epoch Wars](https://cardaniatst.wpenginepowered.com/games/epoch-wars/)
 codex page

Harvesting
----------

You will likely select all tokens available to harvest and the cost for all 40+ tokens will not exceed 1 ADA with current chain TX costs. However, to include all those tokens in the transaction an amount of 7 ADA will be required, so 6 ADA will be returned along with the tokens.
